<script type="text/javascript">
	var hideElementsById = new Array ();
	window.onload = function () {
		if (!hideElementsById || hideElementsById.length < 1)
			return;
		for (index in hideElementsById)
			toggle (hideElementsById [index]);
	}
	
	function toggle (divId)
	{
		var e = document.getElementById (divId);
		if (!e)
			return;
		var h = document.getElementById (divId + "Hint");
		if (e.style.display == "block" || e.style.display == "") {
			e.style.display = "none";
			if (h)
				h.innerHTML = " (click to show)";
		} else {
			e.style.display = "block";
			if (h)
				h.innerHTML = " (click to hide)";
		}
	}
</script>

The authentication information fields provide detailed information about this specific logon request.  	- Transited services indicate which intermediate services have participated in this logon request.  	- Package name indicates which sub-protocol was used among the NTLM protocols.  	- Key length indicates the length of the generated session key. This will be 0 if no session key was requested.

It is generated on the computer where access was attempted.    The Subject fields indicate the account on the local system which requested the logon. The most common types are 2 (interactive) and 3 (network).    The Process Information fields indicate which account and process on the system requested the logon. <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>
<link href="css/main1.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" />

function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;

    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')

	    isIE11 = false;

	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});

function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {

	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});

<p>美丽的珊瑚缸把海底生物养在家里，仿佛人可以每天潜水在海底一样，这是王先生平时生活最大得乐趣，工作之外，他太专注于养硬体珊瑚，以至于在华北地区的珊瑚圈里养出了名堂。</p>\r\n                                                            </div>\r\n                                                            <em class="more"></em>\r\n                                                        </div>\r\n                                                    </a>\r\n                                                   <a  href="/advantage/l1045544.html" target="_blank" class="wid_all">\r\n                                                        <div class="txt">\r\n                                                            <h3 class="ellipsis font-30">尚层装饰“与你的再一次相遇”</h3>\r\n                                                            <div class="c">\r\n                                                                <p>人生数十年，会认识很多新朋友。有些朋友从你人生路过，有些人在你的生命中留下。六年，从纯粹的工作关系变成亲密的朋友。相遇、相知，一起走进设计师张萍的别墅故事 “与你的再一次相遇”</p>\r\n         </div>\r\n                                                    <a  href="/advantage/l1045688.html" target="_blank" class="wid_all">\r\n                                                        <div class="txt">\r\n                                                            <h3 class="ellipsis font-30">李楠的家，李楠的海</h3>\r\n                                                            <div class="c">\r\n                                                                <p>“自己做了这么多年的设计，敢像李楠这么做的，他是第一个。” 像托尔金小说中霍比特人的居所一般，李楠家的客厅，拜占庭式拱形顶上悬下一簇灯光算不上耀眼的银质吊灯，陶土砖墙前面摆着上等牛皮做成的咖色沙发，与华丽二字不沾边，却质朴而考究。 </p>\r\n                                                            </div>\r\n                                                            <em class="more"></em>\r\n                                                        </div>\r\n                                                    </a>\r\n                                                </div>\r\n                                            </li>\r\n onerror="lod(this)"></a>\r\n                                                    </div>\r\n                                                    <a  href="/advantage/l1045657.html" target="_blank" class="wid_all">\r\n                                                        <div class="txt">\r\n                                                            <h3 class="ellipsis font-30">业主评价的&quot;设计&quot; _粗茶淡饭总相宜</h3>\r\n                                                            <div class="c">\r\n                                                                <p>之前有过一次装修经验，找的是普通装修公司。装修过程中有很多的纰漏，交房后的后期维护工作也做得不到位，因此这次新房的装修下决心要找一家专业的公司。与房产商合作的装修公司举办的活动酒会上，我们在现场交了一部分装修定金。但是之后与其设计师沟通后对其装修设计并不是很满意，因此萌生了再找几家装修公司对比的想法。</p>\r\n 		{

			{

            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }

                DownPluginTip = function () {

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>

<script src="js/common.js" type="text/javascript"></script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>
<link href="css/main1.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" />
</head>
<body onselectstart="return fbd();" onresize="ReSize()">
<iframe onload="" id="cgiframe" style="display:none"></iframe>
<iframe onload="" id="cgiframe1" style="display:none"></iframe>

function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});

function ReSize(){}

	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		}

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.1"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>

function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.2"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.2"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.2"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
</script>
<link href="css/main1.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" />

function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.2"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;

	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});

				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){

                    break;

                DownPluginTip = function () {

                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');

			//设计最小值
			onReSize();

		}

		Logout();

	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}

			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){

			    }else{

			    }
            }
        }
        else {

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.2"

    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');

    }

			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{

			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version

                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;

function doEvent(){}
function ReSize(){}
$(function(){
    var isIE11 = true;
    var pVersion = "3.0.0.2"
    var s = navigator.userAgent.split("Trident");
    if (typeof s[1] == 'undefined')
    {
	    isIE11 = false;
    }
	function DownPluginTip(){}
	var isIE = true;
	if (($.browser.safari || $.browser.mozilla) && !isIE11){
		isIE = false;
		doEvent=doEvent1;
		ReSize = function(){try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}}/*chrome有点格鲁*/
		var plugins = navigator.plugins;
		var plugin = false;
		for (var pi = 0; pi  < plugins.length; pi++)
		{
			if (plugins[pi][0].type == "application/ipcam-regplugin")
			{
				vsIf = plugins[pi].description.split("-");
				if (vsIf.length==2) vsIf=vsIf[1];
				else vsIf="";
				plugin = true;break;
			}
		}
		if(!plugin){
		    DownPluginTip = function(){
			    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
			    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
			    if(/firefox/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else if(/chrome/i.test(browserName)){
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ") + '</a>';
			    }else{
				    obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">'+lg.get("IDS_LOGIN_KJ")+'</a>';
			    }
            }
        }
        else {
            //check plugin version
            var v1 = vsIf.split(".");   //plugin version
            var v2 = pVersion.split(".");    //web version
            var needUpdate = false;
            for(var m = 0; m < 4; m++){
                if(v2[m] * 1 > v1[m] * 1){
                    needUpdate = true;
                    break;
                }else if(v2[m] * 1 == v1[m] * 1){
                    continue;
                }else{
                    needUpdate = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (needUpdate) {
                DownPluginTip = function () {
                    var browserName = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                    var obj = document.getElementById("downPlugins");
                    if (/firefox/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else if (/chrome/i.test(browserName)) {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="IPCWebComponents.exe">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    } else {
                        obj.innerHTML = '<a id="down" href="plugins.pkg">' + lg.get("IDS_PLUGIN_UPDATE_TIP") + '</a>';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

		var str="";
		for(var i=0; i<9; i++){
            str += ('<div id="ipcamdiv' + i + '" style="float:left;height:0%;width:0%;"><embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="IPCWebComponents.exe" type="application/ipcam-regplugin" id="ipcam" name="' + i + '"></embed></div>')
		}
		$("#plugin").html(str);
		//$("#plugin").html('<embed width="100%" height="100%" pluginspage="plugins.crx" type="application/ipcam-plugin" id="ipcam"></embed>');
	}else if($.browser.msie || isIE11){
		doEvent=doEvent2;
		if($.browser.version == "6.0"){
			//设计最小值
			onReSize();
			document.body.onresize = function(){onReSize();changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};	
		}else{
			document.body.onresize = function(){changPlugin();try{$("#gsliderCov").trigger("sChange");}catch(e){}};
		}
	}
	window.onbeforeunload = function(e){
		Logout();
	}
	WebInit(DownPluginTip, isIE);
});
